  <o:AllowPNG/>
 </o:OfficeDocumentSettings>
</xml><![endif]--></p>
<p>&nbsp;<span style="font-size: 18pt;"><b><span style="line-height: 115%; mso-fareast-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 18.0pt;"><span style="font-family: Calibri;" face="Calibri">Spiritual Message for the Day â€“ Sadhana â€“ The Main Purpose of Life by Sri Swami Sivananada</span></span></b></span></p>
<p><strong><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Baba Times DigestÂ© |&nbsp;26 July 2014 15.16 EST | New York Edition</span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span><span style="color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><br style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;" /></span></span></strong></p>
<p><strong><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"></span></span></span></strong><hr />
<p style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;<span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="Calibri">Sadhana â€“ The Main Purpose of Life</span></b></span></p>
<p><span style="color: black; font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial;"></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="Calibri">Divine Life Society Publication: </span></b><a href="http://www.sivanandaonline.org/public_html/?cmd=displaysection&amp;section_id=535&amp;format=html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: #0000ff;" color="#0000ff" face="Calibri">Sadhana â€“ The Main Purpose of Life</span></b></a><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="Calibri"> by Sri Swami Sivananda</span></b></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Sadhana means any spiritual practice that helps the aspirant to realise God. It is a means to attain the goal of human life. Sadhana is steadying the mind and fixing it on the Lord. </span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Everyone must take to some kind of Sadhana to attain the state of final beatitude.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Sadhana is the real wealth. It is the only thing of real and everlasting value. There is butter in milk, but it can be got only after churning. Similarly if you want to realise God, do Sadhana and worship constantly in right earnest.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Whatever spiritual practice you do, either Japa, practice of Asanas, meditation or Pranayama, do it systematically and regularly every day. You will attain immortality or eternal bliss.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">If your persist in your Sadhana vigorously and diligently, if you are regular, systematic and punctual in your Sadhana, you will attain success.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Be contented with whatever you get by chance and apply yourself to Sadhana with a dispassionate mind.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Regularity in Sadhana is of paramount importance. He who meditates regularly gets Samadhi quickly. That man who is irregular and does his actions by fits and starts cannot reap the fruits of his efforts.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Keep your mind always busy in doing Japa, concentration, meditation, study of religious books, Satsanga or in doing something useful to others.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Little acts of virtues, little acts of purity will help you a lot in your Sadhana. Removal of Vrittis and impurities is the most important Sadhana. The wandering mind must be controlled by sticking to one place, one preceptor and one progressive method of Sadhana.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">That Sadhaka who has turned the mind inward by the practice of Sama and Dama and who has keen longing for liberation sees the Self in his own Self by constant and deep meditation.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">You can move the whole world by your spiritual force.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">A spiritual diary is a whip for goading the mind towards righteousness.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Selfishness retards spiritual progress. If anyone can destroy his selfishness, half of his spiritual Sadhana is over.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">You must get up at 4 a.m. and start meditation. Have concrete meditation in the beginning. Feel the indwelling presence of God in the form and think of the attributes-purity, perfection, all-pervading intelligence, bliss absolute, omnipotence, etc. When the mind runs again and again bring it to the point. Have another sitting for meditation at night. Be regular in your practice.</span></span>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><span face="Times New Roman"> </span><span face="Calibri">Write your Ishta Mantra in a notebook for one hour daily. Discipline the senses. Observe the vow of silence. Develop right thinking, right feeling, right acting and right speaking. Eradicate vicious qualities, such as anger, lust, greed, egoism, hatred, etc. He who regulates his life on the above lines, is sure to attain success in this very birth, nay, in this very second.</span><span face="Times New Roman"><br /></span></span>
<p style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: left; line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><span face="Calibri"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;" color="#0000ff">&nbsp;</span></span><span style="color: #0000ff;" color="#0000ff">Excerpts from:</span></span></span></b></span></p>
<span style="color: black; font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial;">
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;"><a href="http://www.sivanandaonline.org/public_html/?cmd=displaysection&amp;section_id=535&amp;format=html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: #0000ff;" color="#0000ff" face="Calibri">Sadhana â€“ The Main Purpose of Life</span></b></a><span face="Calibri"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> by Sri Swami Sivananda</b> </span></p>
</span>
<p><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="article_default" style="text-align: left;">&nbsp;</p>
<p><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt;"></span><hr />

<p class="article_default" style="text-align: center;"><hr />
